     <script>
      if( window.location.hostname.indexOf('publico.pt') != -1 ) {
	  var deferredScripts = window.deferredScripts || [];
	  deferredScripts.push(function(){
	    initBarraCoronavirus();
	  });
	} else {
	  $(function(){
	    initBarraCoronavirus();
	  });
	}

	var articleListAPI = {
	  config: {
	  	debugEndpoint: 'https://secret-ocean-49799.herokuapp.com/',
	    endPoint: '/api/list/',
	    endpointLiveBlog: 'https://api.publico.pt/liveblog/',
	    statsEndpoint: 'https://static.publico.pt/files/widgets/covid/highlights/covid-highlights.js',
	    redirectUrl: 'https://www.publico.pt/'
	  },
	  init: function(tag) {
	  	// Get latest live update
	    var endPoint = articleListAPI.config.endPoint + tag;

	    articleListAPI.getArticles(endPoint, tag);

	    // Get COVID numbers
	    var cacheBustTime = new Date();
	    var day = cacheBustTime.getDate();
	    var month = cacheBustTime.getMonth() + 1;
	    month = (month > 9 ? month : '0' + month);

	    var hours = cacheBustTime.getHours();
	    hours = (hours > 9 ? hours : '0' + hours);

	    var minutes = cacheBustTime.getMinutes();
	    minutes = '' + minutes;
	    minutes = minutes.charAt(0);

	    cacheBustTime = '?cachebuster=' + day + month + hours + minutes;

	    var endPoint = articleListAPI.config.statsEndpoint + cacheBustTime;

	    articleListAPI.getStats(endPoint);
	  },
	  getArticles: function(endPoint, tag) {
	    // Article list HTML will be stored in this array
	    var articleListHTML = [];

	    $.get(endPoint, function(articles) {
			var articleId = articles[0].id;
			var articleURL = articles[0].url;

			$('#main').find('.item--live a').attr('href', articleURL);

			tag = articleId + '?headlines=true';

			var endpointLiveBlog = articleListAPI.config.endpointLiveBlog + tag;

			$.get(endpointLiveBlog, function(article) {
				var articleTitle = article[0].titulo;
				if(articleTitle.length >= 64) {
					articleTitle = articleTitle.substring(0, 64);
					articleTitle = articleTitle + '...';
				}
				$('#main').find('.item--live .item__description').text(articleTitle);
			});
	    });
	  },
	  getStats: function(endPoint) {
	    $.ajax({
	        type: "GET",
	        url: endPoint,
	        dataType: 'json'
	    }).done(function(result) {
	      var data = result.total[0];

	      // Infections
	      $('#main').find('.item--infections .item__description').html(data.total_infetados + '<span class="sparks dotline-extrathick"></span>');
	      $('#main').find('.item--infections .item__description span').text('{' + data.grafico_infetados + '}');

	      // Deaths
	      $('#main').find('.item--deaths .item__description').text(data.total_mortos);

	      // Vaccination
	      $('#main').find('.item--vaccination .item__description').text(data.percentagem_vacinados + '%');

	      // World
	      $('#main').find('.item--world .item__description').text(data.novos_infetados_mundo);
	    });
	  }
	};

	function initBarraCoronavirus() {
		articleListAPI.init('coronavirus-ao-minuto');

		$('#main').find('.highlight-bar').on('click', 'a', function(){
		  var trackingLabel = $(this).data('tracking');

		  if (typeof Publico !== 'undefined' && Publico && typeof Publico.Track.Event == 'function') { 
		     Publico.Track.Event('coronaBarra-artigos', 'click',  trackingLabel)
		  } else {
		     console.log( 'track: ' +  trackingLabel)
		  } 
		});
	}
     </script>

     <script>
      if( window.location.hostname.indexOf('publico.pt') != -1 ) {
  var deferredScripts = window.deferredScripts || [];
  deferredScripts.push(function(){
    
    initGamesAnalytics();
  });
} else {
  $(function(){
    
    initGamesAnalytics();
  });
}
 

function initGamesAnalytics() {

  
  $('#stack-games').on('click', 'a', function(){
   var trackingLabel = $(this).data('tracking');

   if (typeof Publico !== 'undefined' && Publico && typeof Publico.Track.Event == 'function') { 

      Publico.Track.Event('jogos-barra-hp', 'click',  trackingLabel)
   } else {
      console.log( 'track: ' +  trackingLabel)
   } 
  });
 
}
     </script>

     <script>
      if( window.location.hostname.indexOf('publico.pt') != -1 ) {
	  var deferredScripts = window.deferredScripts || []; 
	  deferredScripts.push(function(){
	    initMeteoHpBar();
	    initMeteoHpBarData();
	  });
	} else {
	  $(function(){
	    initMeteoHpBar();
	    initMeteoHpBarData();
	  });
	}

	
    
	/**/
	function initMeteoHpBar() {
		


		$('#stack-meteo').on('click', 'a', function(){
		  var trackingLabel = $(this).data('tracking');

		  if (typeof Publico !== 'undefined' && Publico && typeof Publico.Track.Event == 'function') { 
		     Publico.Track.Event('barrahp-meteo', 'click',  trackingLabel)
		  } else {
		     console.log( 'track: ' +  trackingLabel)
		  } 
		});
	}
	function initMeteoHpBarData() {



var timeStamp = Date.now();

  $.ajax({
    
    url: 'https://static.publico.pt/files/widget/meteo/datadetailed.js?z='+timeStamp,
    success: function(data){
      meteoItems = JSON.parse(data);

      
      var lisboaObj = meteoItems.filter(obj => {
              return obj.District === 'Lisboa'
            });
      var portoObj = meteoItems.filter(obj => {
              return obj.District === 'Porto'
            });
      var faroObj = meteoItems.filter(obj => {
              return obj.District === 'Faro'
            });
            var lisboaIcon = lisboaObj[0].Icon;
            var lisboaTemp = lisboaObj[0].Temperature;
            var lisboaMin = lisboaObj[0].TemperatureMin;
            var lisboaMax = lisboaObj[0].TemperatureMax;
      		var lisboaText = '';
      		
      		if (typeof lisboaObj[0].TextBody !== 'undefined') {
              lisboaText = lisboaObj[0].TextBody;
            }
            //var lisboaText = lisboaObj[0].TextBody;
            if(lisboaText.length >= 90) {
                lisboaTextTip = lisboaText;
                lisboaText = lisboaText.substring(0, 90);
                lisboaText = lisboaText + '... ';
                lisboaTooltip = $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(1)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p .has-tip').attr('data-toggle');
                $('#'+lisboaTooltip).html(lisboaTextTip);
              } else {
                $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(1)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p .has-tip').remove();
              }
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(1)').find('.stack__slice__item__media').html('<img src="'+lisboaIcon+'" >');
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(1)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp').html(lisboaTemp);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(1)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp-min').html(lisboaMin);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(1)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp-max').html(lisboaMax);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(1)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p').prepend(lisboaText);
            var portoIcon = portoObj[0].Icon;
            var portoTemp = portoObj[0].Temperature;
            var portoMin = portoObj[0].TemperatureMin;
            var portoMax = portoObj[0].TemperatureMax;
            var portoText = '';
      		if (typeof portoObj[0].TextBody !== 'undefined') {
              portoText = portoObj[0].TextBody;
            }
            if(portoText.length >= 90) {
                portoTextTip = portoText;
                portoText = portoText.substring(0, 90); 
                portoText = portoText + '... ';
                portoTooltip = $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(2)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p .has-tip').attr('data-toggle');
                $('#'+portoTooltip).html(portoTextTip);
              } else {
                $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(2)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p .has-tip').remove();
              }
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(2)').find('.stack__slice__item__media').html('<img src="'+portoIcon+'" >');
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(2)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp').html(portoTemp);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(2)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp-min').html(portoMin);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(2)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp-max').html(portoMax);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(2)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p').prepend(portoText);
            var faroIcon = faroObj[0].Icon;
            var faroTemp = faroObj[0].Temperature;
            var faroMin = faroObj[0].TemperatureMin;
            var faroMax = faroObj[0].TemperatureMax;
            //var faroText = faroObj[0].TextBody;
      		var faroText = '';
      		if (typeof faroObj[0].TextBody !== 'undefined') {
              faroText = faroObj[0].TextBody;
            }
            if(faroText.length >= 90) {
                faroTextTip = faroText;
                faroText = faroText.substring(0, 90);
                faroText = faroText + '... ';
                faroTooltip = $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(3)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p .has-tip').attr('data-toggle');
                $('#'+faroTooltip).html(faroTextTip);
              } else {
                $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(3)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p .has-tip').remove();
              }
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(3)').find('.stack__slice__item__media').html('<img src="'+faroIcon+'" >');
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(3)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp').html(faroTemp);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(3)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp-min').html(faroMin);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(3)').find('.stack__slice__item__data .temp-max').html(faroMax);
            $('#stack-meteo').find('.stack__slice__item:nth-of-type(3)').find('.stack__slice__item__content p').prepend(faroText);

    },
    error: function(){
      $('#main').find('.meteo-data').hide();
    }
  });
}
     </script>

     <script>
      var deferredScripts = window.deferredScripts || [];
deferredScripts.push(function(){
  
    var articleListAPI = {
      config: {
        endPoint: '/api/events/live/latests',
        debugEndpoint: 'https://cors-anywhere.herokuapp.com/' + 'https://www.publico.pt/api/events/live/latests',
        redirectUrl: 'https://www.publico.pt/',
        pageNews: 0
      },
      init: function(targetDiv, tag, page) {

        articleListAPI.config.pageNews = articleListAPI.config.pageNews + 1;
        var page = articleListAPI.config.pageNews;

        articleListAPI.config.articleLimit = 0;

        var endPoint = articleListAPI.config.endPoint;

        articleListAPI.getArticles(targetDiv, endPoint);
      },
      getArticles: function(targetDiv, endPoint) {
        var $targetDiv = $(targetDiv);

        // Article list HTML will be stored in this array
        var articleListHTML = [];

        var wrapperHTML = [];
        articleListHTML.push(wrapperHTML.join(''));

        $.get(endPoint, function(articles) {
            var articleLimit = articleListAPI.config.articleLimit;
            var articleLimitReached = false;

            $.each(articles, function(i, e) {
                if(articleLimit != false && articleLimitReached == false) {
                    if(i >= articleLimit) {
                        articleLimitReached = true;
                    }
                }

                if(articleLimitReached == false) {
                    // Article main details
                    var articleURL      = this.url;
                    var articleTitle    = this.titulo;

                    // Article image
                    var articleImage = '';
                    if(this.multimediaPrincipal != null) {
                      articleImage = '<img src="' + this.multimediaPrincipal + '">';
                    } else if(this.imagens[0].url != null) {
                      articleImage = '<img src="' + this.imagens[0].url + '">';
                    }
					
					// Article Kicker
					var articleKicker='';
					
					if (this.tags && this.tags.length > 0) {
						articleKicker = this.tags[0].nome;
						}else{
						articleKicker = '';
					}
					//if (this.tags.length === 0) {					
						//if(this.tags[0].nome != null) {
						//	articleKicker = this.tags[0].nome
						//	}						
					//}


                    var currentArticleHTML = [
                        '<li class="stack__slice__item">',
                            '<article class="card card--xs tone--news" data-main-element-id="">',
                                '<div class="card__inner">',
                                    '<figure class="card__media">','<div class="flex-media">','<img data-src="'+articleImage+'&amp;w=320&amp;h=180&amp;act=cropResize" data-srcset="'+articleImage+"&amp;w=1600&amp;h=900&amp;act=cropResize 1600w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=1520&amp;h=1140&amp;act=cropResize 1520w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=1280&amp;h=720&amp;act=cropResize 1280w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=908&amp;h=511&amp;act=cropResize 908w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=800&amp;h=450&amp;act=cropResize 800w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=640&amp;h=360&amp;act=cropResize 640w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=454&amp;h=255&amp;act=cropResize 454w, "+articleImage+'&amp;w=320&amp;h=180&amp;act=cropResize 320w" sizes="(min-width: 72.5em) calc(72.5em * 0.5), (min-width: 64em) calc(1 * ((100vw*0.5)-1em)), (min-width: 40em) 78.125vw, 100vw" src="'+articleImage+'&amp;w=320&amp;h=180&amp;act=cropResize" srcset="'+articleImage+"&amp;w=1600&amp;h=900&amp;act=cropResize 1600w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=1520&amp;h=1140&amp;act=cropResize 1520w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=1280&amp;h=720&amp;act=cropResize 1280w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=908&amp;h=511&amp;act=cropResize 908w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=800&amp;h=450&amp;act=cropResize 800w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=640&amp;h=360&amp;act=cropResize 640w, "+articleImage+"&amp;w=454&amp;h=255&amp;act=cropResize 454w, "+articleImage+'&amp;w=320&amp;h=180&amp;act=cropResize 320w">',"</div></figure>",
                                    '<div class="card__content">',
									'<div class="card__header">',
									'<h4 class="kicker ">' + articleKicker + '</h4>',
										'<h3 class="card__title headline">',
											'<a href="'+ articleURL + '" class="card__faux-block-link">'+ articleTitle + '</a>',
										'</h3>',
								'</div>',
							'</div>',         			
						'</div>',
					'</article>',
				'</li>'
                    ];
                    

                    articleListHTML.push(currentArticleHTML.join(''));
                }
            });

            wrapperHTML = [];
            articleListHTML.push(wrapperHTML.join(''));

            $targetDiv.append(articleListHTML.join(''));
        });
      }
    };
    
  
    
    articleListAPI.init('#container-aovivo', 'p3cronica', '');
    
  
function waitForEl(selector, callback){
        var poller1 = setInterval(function(){
            $jObject = jQuery(selector);
            if($jObject.length < 1){
                return;
            }
            clearInterval(poller1);
            callback($jObject)
        },100);
    };
    /* */
    /* */
    waitForEl('#megafone-stack .card__faux-block-link', function() {
        
        $('#megafone-stack').on('click', '.card__faux-block-link', function(){
         
           var trackingLabel = $(this).data('tracking');

           if (typeof Publico !== 'undefined' && Publico && typeof Publico.Track.Event == 'function') { 

              Publico.Track.Event('202011-PSUPERIORHPV2', 'click',  trackingLabel)
           } else {
              console.log( 'track: ' +  trackingLabel)
           } 
      }); 
    }); /* wait for el */
    


});
     </script>

     <script>
      function loadEIImage(){
    var localDate = new Date();
    var currentTimeZoneOffsetInHours = localDate.getTimezoneOffset() / 60;
    if(currentTimeZoneOffsetInHours != 0){
      if(currentTimeZoneOffsetInHours<60){
        currentTimeZoneOffsetInHours = Math.abs(currentTimeZoneOffsetInHours);
      }else{
        currentTimeZoneOffsetInHours = -Math.abs(currentTimeZoneOffsetInHours);
      }
      localDate.setTime(localDate.getTime() + (currentTimeZoneOffsetInHours*60*60*1000)); 
    }

    if((localDate.getMonth() == 11 && localDate.getDate() == 25) || (localDate.getMonth() == 0 && localDate.getDate() == 1)){
      localDate.setTime(localDate.getTime() + (-24*60*60*1000)); 
    }

    if(localDate.getHours() < 2){
      localDate.setTime(localDate.getTime() + (-24*60*60*1000)); 
    }

    var imgUrl = "https://imagens9.publico.pt/imagens.aspx/"+ (localDate.getFullYear()) + "/" + ("0" + (localDate.getMonth()+1)).right(2)  + "/" + ("0" + localDate.getDate()).right(2) + "/P1/Publico.jpg?tp=ARQUIVO";

    $("#paperViewer").attr("data-media-viewer", imgUrl).attr("src", imgUrl + "&w=400&h=502&act=cropResize");
    $("#eiDate").html(localDate.getDate() + " de " + monthNames[localDate.getMonth()] + " de " + localDate.getFullYear());
      
      publico.gallery.watch($("#main").find(".stack--print-edition"));
      
  }

    //Hack so we can receive JSONP used con cartao site
    var angular = {
        callbacks: {
            "_0": function (data) {
                if (data && data.length > 0) {
                    var results = [];
                    data.forEach(function (d) {
                        if (d.featured) {
                            results.push(d);
                        }
                    });
                    results = results.length > 2 ? results.slice(0, 2) : results;
                    Publico.Template.process("vantagem", "shared").then(function (tpl) {
                        var template = Handlebars.compile(tpl.html());
                        var $html = template(results);
                        $("#discounts-container").prepend($html);
                        $("#discounts-container").foundation();
                    });
                }
            }
        }
    };

    if (typeof Publico == "object") {
        loadEIImage()
        getPartnerEvents();
        if(typeof window.trackingId != "undefined"){
          $("#subscribe-link").attr("href", $("#subscribe-link").attr("href") + "?trackingId=" + trackingId);
        }        
    } else {
        var deferredScripts = window.deferredScripts || [];
        deferredScripts.push(function () {
            siteControl._newWayPoint($(".stack--print-edition"), function (el) {
                loadEIImage();
                getPartnerEvents();
            });
        });
    }
     </script>

   <script>
    var deferredScripts = window.deferredScripts || [];
    deferredScripts.push(function () {
        if (typeof userOnPage.userGuid != "undefined" && !userOnPage.isSubscriber) {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/api/user/subscription/" + userOnPage.userGuid,
                xhrFields: {
                    withCredentials: true
                }
            }).success(function (data) {
                if (data && data.result) {
                    sessionStorage.clear();
                    sessionStorage.setItem("user_session", JSON.stringify(data.result));
                    localStorage.setItem("subscriber_ads", JSON.stringify({ isSubscriber: true }));
                    document.location.reload();
                }
            });
        }

        if (Publico.Cookies.get("rgpd_cookie") == null) {
            $(".site-message--cookies").show();
            $('#cookie-declaration-toggle').on('click', function () {
                $('#cookie-declaration-toggle').toggleClass('toggled');
                $('#cookie-declaration').toggleClass('expanded');
            });
            $("#accept-cookie").on("click", function () {
                Publico.Cookies.set("rgpd_cookie", 1, 720);
                $(".site-message--cookies").remove();
                var img = document.createElement('img');
                img.src = "https://stream.publico.pt/g.gif?rnd=" + (new Date()).getTime();
            });
        }
    })
   </script>

                try {
                    var jpj = JSON.parse(jp);
                    if (jpj.isSubscriber) {
                        wasSub = true;
                        userOnPage.isSubscriber = true;
                    }
                } catch (e) { }
            }
        } catch (e) { }

                    window.targetAssinante = targetAssinante = "sim";

                subSeccaoSite.push("home");
            }
        } else if ($("#story-body").length > 0) {
            subSeccaoSite.push(pageSection.slug);
            subSeccaoSite.push("artigo");

            subSeccaoSite.push(pageSection.slug);
            subSeccaoSite.push("listagem");

        if ($(".page__menu").length > 0) {
